## 通用接口参数文档
参数  

| 字段 | 类型 | 描述     |
| ---- | ---- | -------- |
| data | json | 查询参数 |

查询参数：
```json
{
    "chartName": "PV",  //图表名称
    "chartType": "line",	//图表类型.可传值table(表格),simple-table(普通表格),retain(留存图),text(文本提),line(折线图),histogram(柱形图),two-axis(双轴图),line-area(面积图)
    "databaseName": "bi",	//数据库名
    "tableName": "view_sdk_app_sdk_web",	//数据表名
    "limit": "10",  //返回数量
    "rollup":0, //通过去掉所有维度实现上卷，用于实现表格中的总计。0：否；1：是。
    "withRollup":0, //通过sql中得roolup实现上卷，用于实现柱状图中的总计。0：否；1：是。
    "retainTimeNum": "1,2,3",   //留存图距起始时间间隔，多个用逗号分隔。
    "dimension": [
        {
            "name": "date",	//维度名称
            "group": "day",	//聚合粒度。仅时间类型维度可以使用。可传值year、month、week、day、hour
     		"aliasName": "年份", //维度别名
            "order": 0, //排序，默认升序。0：升序；-1：降序；-2：不参与排序。
            "orderContentList":["当日","1天","2~3天"], //自定义排序。
            "groupDataOrderContentList":["新用户","老用户"], //图例自定义排序。
     		"is_column": false, //是否行专列
            "format":"", //维度格式化。"Y-w"：第几周，"Y-w-d"：周区间。
            "havingLogic":"", //sql中的having功能。可传值 eq: 等于; neq: 不等于。
            "havingValue":"" //值
        }
    ],
    "measure": [
        {
            "name": "uv",	//度量名称
            "func": "uniqArray",	//聚合函数。可传count、count_distinct、sum、avg、max、min、uniqArray等
			"aliasName": "网吧", //度量别名
            "order": 0, //排序，默认升序。0：升序；-1：降序；-2：不参与排序。
            "orderContentList":["当日","1天","2~3天"], //自定义排序。
			"minvalue": null, //结果筛选最小值(null为自动)
            "maxvalue": null, //结果筛选最大值(null为自动)
            "digitDisplay": "", //数值显示。percent:百分数显示，保留2位小数。
            "decimal": 3,   //保留小数位数
            "proportion" : 0,   //计算占比。0：否；1：是。
			"contrast": "mom", //高级计算
			/*
			('d_yoy', '昨日同比'), ('w_yoy', '上周同比'), ('m_yoy', '上月同比'), ('y_yoy', '上年同比'),
			('d_yoy_rate', '昨日同比增长率'), ('w_yoy_rate', '上周同比增长率'), ('m_yoy_rate', '上月同比增长率'), ('y_yoy_rate', '上年同比增长率'),
			('mom', '环比'), ('mom_rate', '环比增长率'),
			('d_yoy_value', '昨日同期'), ('w_yoy_value', '上周同期'), ('m_yoy_value', '上月同期'), ('y_yoy_value', '上年同期')
            ('yoy', '同比'),('yoy_rate', '同比增长率')
			*/
        }
    ],
    "dashboard": [{	//全局筛选，针对全部图表。
        "name" : "date",	//全局筛选字段名称
        "logic": "between",	//筛选条件。in: 包含; notin: 不包含; eq: 等于; neq: 不等于;like: 包含; notlike: 不包含; startswith: 开头包含; endswith: 结尾包含;gt: 大于; gte: 大于等于; lt: 小于; lte: 小于等于; between: 区间；isnull: name is null; isblank: name = ''; isempty: name is null or name = ''; isnotnull:name is not null; isnotblank: name != '';isnotempty:name is not null and name != '';
        "value": "lastThirtyDays",	//值。logic是in、between时值为数组,logic是eq时值为普通字符串和数字
        "func": "day"	//函数(仅日期类型字段用)。可传值year(年),month(月),day(日),hour(时),minute(分)
		/*
		 日期类型字段动态条件如下
		今天：logic传eq，value传today
		昨天：logic传eq，value传yesterday
		本周:logic传between，value传thisWeek
		上周:logic传between，value传lastWeek
		本月:logic传between，value传thisMonth
		上月:logic传between，value传lastMonth
		近7天:logic传between，value传inSevenDays
		过去7天：logic传between，value传lastSevenDays
		近30天:logic传between，value传inThirtyDays
		过去30天:logic传between，value传lastThirtyDays
		近90天:logic传between，value传inNinetyDays
		过去90天:logic传between，value传lastNinetyDays
		近15天:logic传between，value传inFifteenDays
		过去15天:logic传between，value传lastFifteenDays
		*/
    }],
    "screen": [{	//图内筛选，针对当前图表。传值逻辑同全局筛选。
        "name" : "channel",
        "empty" : null,
        "logic": "eq",
        "value": "aa",
        "func": ""
    }],
    "compare": [{	//对比条件。传值逻辑同全局筛选。
        "name" : "date",
        "logic": "between",
        "value": "lastThirtyDays",
        "func": "day"
    }]
}
```
## 产品线下拉选项
- 查询参数：
    ```json
    {
        "chartType": "simple-table",
        "databaseName": "bi",
        "tableName": "product",
        "dimension": [],
        "measure": [
            {
                "name": "sdk_product_name",
                "contrast": ""
            },{
                "name": "product_id",
                "contrast": ""
            },{
                "name": "product_name",
                "contrast": ""
            }
        ],
        "dashboard": [{
            "name" : "is_valid",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "1",
            "func": ""
        }],
        "screen": []
    }
    ```
    
- 使用说明
    product_name用于界面展示，product_id作为筛选条件
## 数据概况
### 媒体商下拉选项
查询参数：
```json
{
    "chartType": "simple-table",
    "databaseName": "bi",
    "tableName": "view_sdk_app_sdk_web_register_info",
    "dimension": [],
    "measure": [
        {
            "name": "agent_name",
            "func": "distinct",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "媒体商"
        }
    ],
    "dashboard": [
        {
            "name": "product",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "",
            "注释": "全局筛选，产品线。"
        },
        {
            "name": "date",
            "logic": "between",
            "value": [
                "2020-09-27",
                "2020-09-27"
            ],
            "func": "day",
            "注释": "全局筛选，时间。"
        }
    ],
    "screen": []
}
```
### 子渠道下拉选项
查询参数：
```json
{
    "chartType": "simple-table",
    "databaseName": "bi",
    "tableName": "view_sdk_app_sdk_web_register_info",
    "dimension": [],
    "measure": [
        {
            "name": "channel_name",
            "func": "distinct",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "子渠道"
        }
    ],
    "dashboard": [
        {
            "name": "product",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "",
            "注释": "全局筛选，产品线。"
        },
        {
            "name": "date",
            "logic": "between",
            "value": [
                "2020-09-27",
                "2020-09-27"
            ],
            "func": "day",
            "注释": "全局筛选，时间。"
        }
    ],
    "screen": [
        {
            "name": "agent_name",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "",
            "注释": "所选媒体商"
        }
    ]
}
```
### 活动策略下拉选项
查询参数：
```json
{
    "chartType": "simple-table",
    "databaseName": "bi",
    "tableName": "view_sdk_app_sdk_web_register_info",
    "dimension": [],
    "measure": [
        {
            "name": "cid_name",
            "func": "distinct",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "活动策略"
        }
    ],
    "dashboard": [
        {
            "name": "product",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "",
            "注释": "全局筛选，产品线。"
        },
        {
            "name": "date",
            "logic": "between",
            "value": [
                "2020-09-27",
                "2020-09-27"
            ],
            "func": "day",
            "注释": "全局筛选，时间。"
        }
    ],
    "screen": [
        {
            "name": "agent_name",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "",
            "注释": "所选媒体商"
        },
        {
            "name": "channel_name",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "",
            "注释": "所选子渠道"
        }
    ]
}
```

- 动态度量
  - 点击访客数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "visitor",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName":"游客数"
    }
    ``` 
  - 点击注册数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "register_user",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName":"注册数"
    },
    {
        "name": "uniqArrayIf(register_user, notEmpty(register_user)) / uniqArrayIf(uv, notEmpty(uv))",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName":"注册转化率"
    }
    ```
  - 点击新付费数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "length(arrayIntersect(groupArrayArray(register_user), groupArrayArray(pay_user)))",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName":"新付费数"
    },
    {
        "name": "length(arrayIntersect(groupArrayArray(register_user), groupArrayArray(pay_user))) / uniqArray(register_user)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "新付费转化率"
    }
    ```

## 渠道数据
### 数据趋势
- 查询参数：
    ```json
        {
            "id": "channelAnalysis-0",
            "chartName": "数据趋势",
            "chartType": "line",
            "databaseName": "bi",
            "tableName": "view_sdk_app_sdk_web",
            "dimension": [
                {
                    "name": "agent_name",
                    "group": "",
                    "aliasName": "媒体商",
                    "注释": "汇总维度选中媒体商，aliasName为媒体商,name为agent_name；选中子渠道，aliasName为子渠道，name为channel_name；选中活动策略，aliasName为活动策略，name为cid_name；选中计费名，aliasName为计费名，name为billing_name。"
                }
            ],
            "measure": [
                {
                    "name": "uv",
                    "func": "uniqArray",
                    "contrast": "",
                    "aliasName": "访客数(UV)"
                }
            ],
            "dashboard": [],
            "screen": []
        }
    ```
- 全局筛选：
    | 名称       | 字段名      | 说明                                       |
    | ---------- | ----------- | ------------------------------------------ |
    | 产品       | product     |                                            |
    | 日期       | date        | 参考dashboard参数日期传值说明              |
- 动态参数:    
    >选中指标为浏览量(PV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "pv",
        "func": "sum",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访客数(UV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "uv",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访客数(UV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访问次数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "start_sessions",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访问次数"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问时长(m)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "(sum(online_duration) / uniqArray(start_sessions))/60000",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问时长(m)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问深度，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(pv) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问深度"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均页面停留时长(m)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "(sum(online_duration)/sum(pv))/60000",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均页面停留时长(m)"
    }
    ```

    ```json
            },
    ```

    ```json
                "name": "original_channel_pay_user",
                "func": "uniqArray",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "付费用户数",
                "order": -1
            },
            {
                "name": "original_channel_pay_fee_sum",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "付费总金额",
                "order": -1
            },
            {
                "name": "sum(original_channel_pay_fee_sum) / uniqArrayIf(original_channel_pay_user, notEmpty(original_channel_pay_user))",
                "func": "",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "付费ARPU",
                "order": -1
            }
        ],
        "dashboard": [{
            "name": "date",
            "olapType": "DATE",
            "logic": "between",
            "value": null,
            "func": "day"
        }],
    ```

### 活跃留存
- 查询参数
    ```json
    {
        "id": "channelAnalysis-40",
        "chartName": "活跃留存",
        "chartType": "retain-line-total",
        "databaseName": "bi",
        "tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d",
        "dimension": [
            {
                "name": "reg_date",
                "group": "",
                "aliasName": "起始时间"
            },
            {
                "name": "intervals",
                "group": "",
                "aliasName": "距起始时间间隔"
            },
            {
                "name": "agent_name",
                "group": "",
                "aliasName": "媒体商",
                "注释": "汇总维度选中媒体商，aliasName为媒体商,name为agent_name；选中子渠道，aliasName为子渠道，name为channel_name；选中活动策略，aliasName为活动策略，name为cid_name；选中计费名，aliasName为计费名，name为billing_name。"
            }
        ],
        "measure": [
            {
                "name": "initial_count",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "初始值"
            },
            {
                "name": "retain_count",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "留存值"
            }
        ],
        "dashboard": [{
            "name" : "agg_dim",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "pid:cid",
            "func": ""
        }],
        "screen": [{
            "name" : "user_type",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "reg2active",
            "func": ""
        },{
            "name" : "period_type",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "第n日",
            "func": ""
        },{
            "name" : "intervals",
            "logic": "lte",
            "value": "30",
            "func": ""
        }]
    }
    ```
- 动态条件
    > 切换留存图类型时，chartType会变化。总体留存率（折线图），"chartType": "retain-line-total"；总体留存率（表格图），"chartType": "retain-line-total-table"；留存率变化（折线图）"chartType": "retain-line-change"；留存率变化（表格图）"chartType": "retain-line-change-table"；留存表格"chartType": "retain-table"；

    > 切换留存间隔时，表名和图内筛选器会变化。 
        按日，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"；按周，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_w"，period_type="第n周"；按月，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_m"，period_type="第n月； 
        选中“xy留存”，intervals<=x。举例如下 
        当日留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"，intervals<=0；次日留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"，intervals<=1；
        8周留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_w"，period_type="第n周"，intervals<=8；12月留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_m"，period_type="第n月"，intervals<=12；

    > 留存数。选中3日留存，retainTimeNum="1,2,3";选中6日留存，retainTimeNum="1,2,3,4,5,6";以此类推。    
- 查询结果
    ```json
    
    ```

- 全局筛选：
    | 名称       | 字段名      | 说明                                       |
    | ---------- | ----------- | ------------------------------------------ |
    | 产品       | product     |                                            |
    | 日期       | date        | 参考dashboard参数日期传值说明              |
    |渠道          |channel|      页面调整时传递  |
- 动态参数:    
    >选中指标为浏览量(PV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "pv",
        "func": "sum",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访客数(UV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "uv",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访客数(UV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访问次数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "start_sessions",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访问次数"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问时长，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "(sum(online_duration) / uniqArray(start_sessions))/60000",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问时长(m)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问深度，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(pv) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问深度"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均页面停留时长(m)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "(sum(online_duration)/sum(pv))/60000",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均页面停留时长(m)"
    }
    ```
- 返回结果：

- 动态指标: 
    >选中指标为浏览量(PV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "pv",
        "func": "sum",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访客数(UV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "uv",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访客数(UV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为新访客数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "new_uv",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "新访客数(UV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访问次数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "start_sessions",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访问次数"
    }
    ```
    >人均浏览页数
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(pv)/uniqArray(uv)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "人均浏览页数"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问时长，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(online_duration) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问时长"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问深度，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(pv) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问深度"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为跳出率，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "(countEqual(arrayEnumerateUniq(groupArrayArray(start_sessions)), 1) - countEqual(arrayEnumerateUniq(groupArrayArray(start_sessions)), 2)) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "跳出率"
    }
    ```

- 动态指标: 
    >选中指标为浏览量(PV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "pv",
        "func": "sum",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访客数(UV)，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "uv",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访客数(UV)"
    }
    ```

    ```json
    {
        "name": "new_uv",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "新访客数(UV)"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为访问次数，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "start_sessions",
        "func": "uniqArray",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访问次数"
    }
    ```
    >人均浏览页数
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(pv)/uniqArray(uv)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "人均浏览页数"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问时长，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(online_duration) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问时长"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为平均访问深度，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(pv) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问深度"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为跳出率，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "(countEqual(arrayEnumerateUniq(groupArrayArray(start_sessions)), 1) - countEqual(arrayEnumerateUniq(groupArrayArray(start_sessions)), 2)) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "跳出率"
    }
    ```

    >选中指标为平均访问深度，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(pv) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "平均访问深度"
    }
    ```
    >选中指标为跳出率，度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "(countEqual(arrayEnumerateUniq(groupArrayArray(start_sessions)), 1) - countEqual(arrayEnumerateUniq(groupArrayArray(start_sessions)), 2)) / uniqArray(start_sessions)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "跳出率"
    }
    ```

## 页面分析V2
说明：前端不再需要传递一大串json。只需要传递以下固定参数。
|  参数   | 描述  |
|  ----  | ----  |
| id  | 请求图表标识 |
| product  | 产品 |
| startDate  | 开始时间 |
| endDate  | 结束时间 |
| group  | 聚合粒度。年：year；月：month；日：day。 |
| agentName  | 媒体商 |
| channelName  | 子渠道 |
| cidName  | 活动策略 |
| billingName  | 计费名 |
| userType  | 用户类型。老访客：0；新访客：1；会员：2。 |
| osType  | 终端类型。multiIf(os_type = 1, 'Web', os_type = 7, 'PC', os_type = 4, 'H5', os_type = 2, 'iOS', os_type = 3, 'Android', os_type = 6, '微信小程序', os_type = 8, '微信小游戏', os_type = 9, 'TV', 'other') |
| url  | 联动或展开时点击的url |
### PC端
#### 总览
- 查询参数
    ```json
    {
        "id": "sdk-pageAnalysis-v2-visitPage-overview",
        "chartName": "总览",
        "chartType": "table",
        "databaseName": "banyan_bi_sdk",
        "tableName": "view_sdk_app_sdk_web_session",
        "dimension": [
        ],
        "measure": [
            {
                "name": "pv",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)",
                "order": -1
            },
            {
                "name": "count(distinct uv)",
                "func": "",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "访客数(UV)",
                "order": -1
            },
            {
                "name": "count(distinct if(user_type=0,uv,null))",
                "func": "",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "老访客数",
                "order": -1
            },
            {
                "name": "count(distinct if(user_type=1,uv,null))",
                "func": "",
                "contrast": "",

                "order": -1

                "order": -1

                "order": -1

            },
            {
                "name": "countIf(max_page_sequence=page_sequence and page_sequence = 1 and in_time < subtractMinutes(now(), 30)) / count(distinct session)",
                "func": "",
                "contrast": "",

                "decimal": 2,
                "order": -1
            }
        ],
        "dashboard": [

                "value": 320000,

            },
            {
                "name": "cid_name",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": null,
                "func": "",
                "注释": "全局筛选，活动策略。"
            },
            {
                "name": "billing_name",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": null,
                "func": "",
                "注释": "全局筛选，计费名。"
            },
            {
    ```

#### 访问页面明细
##### 数据趋势
- 说明
    选中浏览量(PV),度量为
    ```json
     {
        "name": "pv",
        "func": "sum",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)"
    }
    ```
    选中下游贡献量,度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(if(max_page_sequence>page_sequence, 1, 0))",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "下游贡献量"
    }
    ```    
    选中访问次数,度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "count(distinct session)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访问次数"
    }
    ```    
    选中访客(UV),度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct uv)",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "访客(UV)"
        }
    ```        
    选中老访客数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct if(user_type=0,uv,null))",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "老访客数"
        }
    ```        
    选中新访客数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct if(user_type=1,uv,null))",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "新访客数"
        }
    ```        
    选中活跃用户数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct active_user)",

            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "活跃用户数"
        }
    ```            
    选中IP数,度量为
    ```json
        {

            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "IP数"
        }
    ```

    ```json

        }
    ```      

##### 数据明细                              
- 查询参数
    ```json
    {
        "id": "sdk-pageAnalysis-v2-pageDetail-10",
        "chartName": "数据趋势",
        "chartType": "table",

        "tableName": "view_sdk_app_sdk_web_session",
        "dimension": [
            {
                "name": "date",
                "group": "day",
                "aliasName": "时间"
            },
            {
                "name": "page_url",
                "group": "",
                "aliasName": "页面url"
            }
        ],
        "measure": [
            {
                "name": "pv",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)"
            },
            {
                "name": "sum(if(max_page_sequence>page_sequence, 1, 0))",
                "func": "",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "下游贡献量"
            },
            {
                "name": "count(distinct session)",
                "func": "",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "访问次数"
            },
            {
                "name": "count(distinct uv)",
                "func": "",
    ```             

#### 访问页面明细
##### 数据趋势
- 说明
    选中浏览量(PV),度量为
    ```json
     {
        "name": "pv",
        "func": "sum",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "浏览量(PV)"
    }
    ```
    选中下游贡献量,度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "sum(if(max_page_sequence>page_sequence, 1, 0))",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "下游贡献量"
    }
    ```    
    选中访问次数,度量为
    ```json
    {
        "name": "count(distinct session)",
        "func": "",
        "contrast": "",
        "aliasName": "访问次数"
    }
    ```    
    选中访客(UV),度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct uv)",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "访客(UV)"
        }
    ```        
    选中老访客数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct if(user_type=0,uv,null))",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "老访客数"
        }
    ```      
    选中新访客数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct if(user_type=1,uv,null))",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "新访客数"
        }
    ```        
    选中活跃用户数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct active_user)",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "活跃用户数"
        }
    ```            
    选中IP数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "count(distinct ip)",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "IP数"
        }
    ```                  
    选中平均页面停留时长(m),度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "sum(online_duration) / 60000 / sum(pv)",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "平均页面停留时长(m)",
            "decimal": 2
        }
    ```      
    选中退出次数,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "countIf(max_page_sequence=page_sequence and in_time < subtractMinutes(now(), 30))",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "退出次数"
        }
    ```  
    选中退出率,度量为
    ```json
        {
            "name": "countIf(max_page_sequence=page_sequence and in_time < subtractMinutes(now(), 30)) / sum(pv)",
            "func": "",
            "contrast": "",
            "aliasName": "退出率",
            "decimal": 2
        }
    ```

## 用户分析
### 用户生命周期
#### 全局筛选
| 名称       | 字段名      | 说明                                       |
| ---------- | ----------- | ------------------------------------------ |
| 产品       | product_id     |                                            |
#### 新手阶段-总用户数

    ```json

        "chartType": "text",

                "aliasName": "日期"
            }
    ```

### 用户留存

| ---------- | ----------- | ------------------------------------------ |

| 日期       | reg_date        | 参考dashboard参数日期传值说明              |
| 渠道   |      |                                            |

##### 活跃留存    
- 查询参数
    ```json
    {
        "id": "sdk-userAnalysis-userRetain-active-40",
        "chartName":"活跃留存",
        "chartType": "retain-line-total",

        "tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d",
        "dimension": [
            {
                "name": "reg_date",
                "group": "",

                "name": "intervals",
                "group": "",
                "aliasName": "距起始时间间隔"
            }
        ],

            {
                "name": "initial_count",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "初始值"
            },
            {
                "name": "retain_count",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",

            },

                "func": "",
                "注释": "全局筛选，计费名。"
            }
        ],
        "screen": [{
            "name" : "user_type",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "reg2active",
            "func": ""
        },{
            "name" : "period_type",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "第n日",
            "func": ""
        },{
            "name" : "intervals",
            "logic": "lte",
            "value": "30",
            "func": ""
        }]
    }
    ```
- 动态条件
    > 切换留存图类型时，chartType会变化。总体留存率（折线图），"chartType": "retain-line-total"；总体留存率（表格图），"chartType": "retain-line-total-table"；留存率变化（折线图）"chartType": "retain-line-change"；留存率变化（表格图）"chartType": "retain-line-change-table"；留存表格"chartType": "retain-table"；

    > 切换留存间隔时，表名和图内筛选器会变化。 
        按日，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"；按周，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_w"，period_type="第n周"；按月，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_m"，period_type="第n月； 
        选中“xy留存”，intervals<=x。举例如下 
        当日留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"，intervals<=0；次日留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"，intervals<=1；
        8周留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_w"，period_type="第n周"，intervals<=8；12月留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_m"，period_type="第n月"，intervals<=12；

    > 留存数。选中3日留存，retainTimeNum="1,2,3";选中6日留存，retainTimeNum="1,2,3,4,5,6";以此类推。

- 查询结果
    ```json
    {
        "code": 20000,
        "status": "success",
        "data": {
            "limit": null,
            "total": null,
            "sql": "select `intervals` as dimension0, sum(`retain_count`) / sum(`initial_count`) as measure0 from bi.dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d where (1 = 1 and intervals <= ? and `agg_dim` in (?, ?, ?)) group by `intervals` order by dimension0 asc, measure0 asc limit 500 offset 0",
            "bindValues": [
                "30",
                "day:product_id:channel_id",
                "week:product_id:channel_id",
                "month:product_id:channel_id"
            ],
            "cacheHit": false,
            "datasTime": null,
            "datas": [
                {
                    "category": "dimension",
                    "group": "",
                    "name": "intervals",
                    "displayName": "intervals",
                    "data": [
                    ],
                    "order": null,
                    "format": null,
                    "distinctData": null
                },
                {
                    "data": [
                    ],
                    "category": "measure",
                    "displayName": "sum(`retain_count`) / sum(`initial_count`)",
                    "name": "sum(`retain_count`) / sum(`initial_count`)",
                    "type": null,
                    "order": null,
                    "contrast": null,
                    "summary": null,
                    "groupData": null,
                    "dimensionData": null
                }
            ]
        }
    }

    ```

##### 付费留存
- 查询参数
    ```json
    {
        "id": "sdk-userAnalysis-userRetain-pay-90",
        "chartName":"付费留存",
        "chartType": "retain-line-total",
        "databaseName": "bi",
        "tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d",
        "dimension": [
            {
                "name": "reg_date",
                "group": "",
                "aliasName": "起始时间"
            },
            {
                "name": "intervals",
                "group": "",
                "aliasName": "距起始时间间隔"
            }
        ],
        "measure": [
            {
                "name": "initial_count",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "初始值"
            },
            {
                "name": "retain_count",
                "func": "sum",
                "contrast": "",
                "aliasName": "留存值"
            }
        ],
        "dashboard": [
            {
                "name": "agg_dim",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": "pid:cid",
                "func": ""
            },
            {
                "name": "product_id",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": 120600
            },
            {
                "name": "reg_date",
                "logic": "between",
                "value": [
                    "2020-08-30",
                    "2020-09-28"
                ]
            },
            {
                "name": "agent_name",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": null,
                "func": "",
                "注释": "全局筛选，媒体商。"
            },
            {
                "name": "channel_name",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": null,
                "func": "",
                "注释": "全局筛选，子渠道。"
            },
            {
                "name": "cid_name",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": null,
                "func": "",
                "注释": "全局筛选，活动策略。"
            },
            {
                "name": "billing_name",
                "logic": "eq",
                "value": null,
                "func": "",
                "注释": "全局筛选，计费名。"
            }
        ],
        "screen": [{
            "name" : "user_type",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "reg2pay",
            "func": ""
        },{
            "name" : "period_type",
            "logic": "eq",
            "value": "第n日",
            "func": ""
        },{
            "name" : "intervals",
            "logic": "lte",
            "value": "30",
            "func": ""
        }]
    }
    ```
- 动态条件
    > 切换留存图类型时，chartType会变化。总体留存率（折线图），"chartType": "retain-line-total"；总体留存率（表格图），"chartType": "retain-line-total-table"；留存率变化（折线图）"chartType": "retain-line-change"；留存率变化（表格图）"chartType": "retain-line-change-table"；留存表格"chartType": "retain-table"；

    > 切换留存间隔时，表名和图内筛选器会变化。 
        按日，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"；按周，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_w"，period_type="第n周"；按月，表名"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_m"，period_type="第n月； 
        选中“xy留存”，intervals<=x。举例如下 
        当日留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"，intervals<=0；次日留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_d"，period_type="第n日"，intervals<=1；
        8周留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_w"，period_type="第n周"，intervals<=8；12月留存，"tableName": "dws_bi_sdk_user_retain_m"，period_type="第n月"，intervals<=12；

    > 留存数。选中3日留存，retainTimeNum="1,2,3";选中6日留存，retainTimeNum="1,2,3,4,5,6";以此类推。
